k3_seed < (1<<20) && !found; k3_seed++) {\n            uint32_t ek3 = expand_table[k3_seed];\n            \n            // Compute L3 for first pair from backward\n            uint32_t L3_0 = R4[0] ^ f_function(L4[0] ^ ek3);\n            \n            // Derive K2\n            // f(L3 ^ K2) = L4 ^ R1 => L3 ^ K2 = f_inv(L4 ^ R1) => K2 = L3 ^ f_inv(L4 ^ R1)\n            uint32_t k2_exp = L3_0 ^ f_inverse(L4[0] ^ R1_fwd_0);\n            \n            // Derive K1\n            // f(R1 ^ K1) = R0' ^ L3 => R1 ^ K1 = f_inv(R0' ^ L3) => K1 = R1 ^ f_inv(R0' ^ L3)\n            uint32_t k1_exp = R1_fwd_0 ^ f_inverse(R0p[0] ^ L3_0);\n            \n            // Check if k2_exp and k1_exp correspond to valid 20-bit seeds\n            // (they must exist in expand_table)\n            // We can check by iterating over all seeds, but that's slow.\n            // Instead, we just verify with all pairs.\n            \n            // Quick verify with first pair\n            uint32_t keys[4] = {ek0, k1_exp, k2_exp, ek3};\n            // Compute encryption of PT[0] with these keys\n            uint32_t left = L0[0];\n            uint32_t right = R0p[0];\n            for (int r = 0; r < 4; r++) {\n                uint32_t mixed = f_function(right ^ keys[r]);\n                uint32_t temp = right;\n                right = left ^ mixed;\n                left = temp;\n            }\n            left ^= right;\n            uint64_t computed_ct = merge(right, left);\n            \n            if (computed_ct == ct[0]) {\n                // Verify with all pairs\n                int ok = 1;\n                for (int p = 0; p < num_pairs && ok; p++) {\n                    left = L0[p];\n                    right = R0p[p];\n                    for (int r = 0; r < 4; r++) {\n                        uint32_t mixed = f_function(right ^ keys[r]);\n                        uint32_t temp = right;\n                        right = left ^ mixed;\n                        left = temp;\n                    }\n                    left ^= right;\n                    uint64_t computed_ct2 = merge(right, left);\n                    if (computed_ct2 != ct[p]) {\n                        ok = 0;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (ok) {\n                    printf(\"\\nFOUND KEYS!\\n\");\n                    printf(\"K0_seed=0x%05X (exp=0x%08X)\\n\", k0_seed, ek0);\n                    \n                    // Find seeds for other keys\n                    printf(\"K1_exp=0x%08X (seed(s): \", k1_exp);\n                    for (int s = 0; s < (1<<20); s++) {\n                        if (expand_table[s] == k1_exp) printf(\"0x%05X \", s);\n                    }\n                    printf(\")\\n\");\n                    \n                    printf(\"K2_exp=0x%08X (seed(s): \", k2_exp);\n                    for (int s = 0; s < (1<<20); s++) {\n                        if (expand_table[s] == k2_exp) printf(\"0x%05X \", s);\n                    }\n                    printf(\")\\n\");\n                    \n                    printf(\"K3_seed=0x%05X (exp=0x%08X)\\n\", k3_seed, ek3);\n                    \n                    // Decrypt ciphertexts\n                    FILE *cfp = fopen(\"/app/ciphertexts.txt\", \"r\");\n                    FILE *ofp = fopen(\"/app/plaintexts.txt\", \"w\");\n                    if (cfp && ofp) {\n                        while (fgets(line, sizeof(line), cfp)) {\n                            unsigned long long c;\n                            if (sscanf(line, \"%llu\", &c) == 1) {\n                                uint64_t ct_val = c;\n                                uint32_t left = getright(ct_val);\n                                uint32_t right = getleft(ct_val);\n                                left ^= right;\n                                for (int r = 3; r >= 0; r--) {\n                                    uint32_t temp = left;\n                                    left = right;\n                                    uint32_t mixed = f_function(temp ^ keys[r]);\n                                    right = temp;\n                                    left ^= mixed;\n                                }\n                                right ^= left;\n                                uint64_t pt_val = merge(left, right);\n                                fprintf(ofp, \"%llu\\n\", (unsigned long long)pt_val);\n                            }\n                        }\n                        fclose(cfp);\n                        fclose(ofp);\n                        printf(\"\\nDecrypted to /app/plaintexts.txt\\n\");\n                    }\n                    found = 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if (!found) {\n        printf(\"Not found!\\n\");\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}\nEOF\ngcc -O3 -o /app/final_attack /app/final_attack.c 2>&1\n",
      "duration": 0.1
    }
  ],
  "task_complete": false
}
```
